# Diagram: research/orchestrator/tasks/transforms/copy_to_redis.py


> Auto-generated by Obscura crawlers

## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start]) --> LoadEnv[Load Environment Variables]
    LoadEnv --> ConnectRedis[Connect to Redis]
    ConnectRedis --> LoopModels{For Each Model}
    LoopModels --> |Next Model| GetModelConfig[Get Model Configuration]
    GetModelConfig --> BuildQuery[Build SQL Query]
    BuildQuery --> InitPagination[Initialize Pagination: last_index=0]
    InitPagination --> QueryLoop{Query Database}
    QueryLoop --> |LIMIT records| ExecuteQuery[Execute SQL Query on SQLite]
    ExecuteQuery --> CheckData{Data Returned?}
    CheckData --> |No Data| NextModel[Next Model]
    CheckData --> |Has Data| UpdateIndex[Update last_index]
    UpdateIndex --> SpecialProcessing{Model Needs Special Processing?}
    SpecialProcessing --> |modelshipmentsplc| ApplyFordOverride[Apply Ford SPLC Override]
    SpecialProcessing --> |No| ProcessRows[Process Rows]
    ApplyFordOverride --> ProcessRows
    ProcessRows --> RowLoop{For Each Row}
    RowLoop --> |Next Row| SkipSubroute{Skip Subroute Missing Data?}
    SkipSubroute --> |Yes| RowLoop
    SkipSubroute --> |No| MapKey[Map Row to Redis Key]
    MapKey --> DetermineValue{Determine Redis Value}
    DetermineValue --> |Ford Override| UseFordValue[Use Override Value]
    DetermineValue --> |Standard| UseModelValue[Use Model Value Field]
    UseFordValue --> BuildDict[Build Value Dictionary]
    UseModelValue --> BuildDict
    BuildDict --> CheckExists{Key Exists in Redis?}
    CheckExists --> |Yes| MergeValues[Merge with Existing Values]
    CheckExists --> |No| SetNew[Create New Value]
    MergeValues --> StoreRedis[Store in Redis]
    SetNew --> StoreRedis
    StoreRedis --> RowLoop
    RowLoop --> |Done| QueryLoop
    NextModel --> LoopModels
    LoopModels --> |All Done| End([End])
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Main
    participant Redis
    participant SQLite
    participant DataFrame
    participant KeyMapper
    
    Main->>Redis: Connect to Redis Host
    Redis-->>Main: Connection Established
    
    loop For Each Model
        Main->>Main: Get Model Configuration
        Main->>SQLite: Query with Pagination
        SQLite-->>DataFrame: Return Records
        
        alt Data Available
            loop While Records Exist
                DataFrame->>Main: Chunk of Records
                
                opt Special Processing
                    Main->>Main: Apply Ford Override Rules
                end
                
                loop For Each Row
                    Main->>KeyMapper: map_row_to_redis_key(field_map, row)
                    KeyMapper->>KeyMapper: normalize_value_string()
                    KeyMapper-->>Main: Redis Key String
                    
                    Main->>Redis: GET existing value
                    Redis-->>Main: Existing Value or None
                    
                    alt Key Exists
                        Main->>Main: Parse JSON and Merge
                    end
                    
                    Main->>Main: Build Final Value Dict
                    Main->>Redis: SET key, json_value
                end
                
                Main->>SQLite: Query next chunk (last_index += size)
                SQLite-->>DataFrame: Return Records
            end
        end
    end
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class ModelConfiguration {
        +String model_name
        +String db_filename
        +List query_fields
        +Dict field_map
        +String value_field
    }
    
    class RedisConnection {
        +String host
        +Int port
        +Int db
        +set(key, value)
        +get(key)
    }
    
    class DataProcessor {
        +normalize_value_string(value) String
        +map_row_to_redis_key(field_map, row) String
        +copy_to_redis(model_version)
    }
    
    class FieldMap {
        +String eta_source
        +String mode_id
        +String dest_id
        +String poi_code
        +String origin_id
        +String next_planned_loc_id
        +String day_of_week
        +String shipment_status_code
    }
    
    class RedisValue {
        +String eta_source
        +Float eta
        +String eta_date
        +String model_version
        +String org_fv_id
    }
    
    ModelConfiguration "1" --> "1" FieldMap: contains
    DataProcessor --> RedisConnection: uses
    DataProcessor --> ModelConfiguration: processes
    DataProcessor --> RedisValue: creates
    RedisConnection --> RedisValue: stores
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
graph LR
    subgraph Input["Data Sources"]
        DB1[(SQLite: model180daystatus.db)]
        DB2[(SQLite: modelentity180daysplc.db)]
        DB3[(SQLite: modelentity180daylatlng.db)]
        DB4[(SQLite: modelshipment180daylatlng.db)]
        DB5[(SQLite: modelshipmentsplc.db)]
        DB6[(SQLite: modelshipmentltl.db)]
        DB7[(SQLite: modelshipmentparcel.db)]
        DB8[(SQLite: model_shipment_ieta_l1_ocean.db)]
        Override[Ford Override CSV]
    end
    
    subgraph Processing["Data Processing Layer"]
        Script[sync.py]
        Norm[normalize_value_string]
        Mapper[map_row_to_redis_key]
    end
    
    subgraph Output["Storage Layer"]
        Redis[(Redis Cache)]
    end
    
    DB1 --> Script
    DB2 --> Script
    DB3 --> Script
    DB4 --> Script
    DB5 --> Script
    DB6 --> Script
    DB7 --> Script
    DB8 --> Script
    Override --> Script
    
    Script --> Norm
    Script --> Mapper
    Norm --> Redis
    Mapper --> Redis
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialize
    Initialize --> ConnectRedis: Load Config
    ConnectRedis --> SelectModel: Connection OK
    
    SelectModel --> LoadModelConfig: Next Model
    LoadModelConfig --> QueryDatabase: Build Query
    
    QueryDatabase --> ProcessChunk: Fetch Records
    ProcessChunk --> CheckEmpty: Parse DataFrame
    
    CheckEmpty --> QueryDatabase: Has More Pages
    CheckEmpty --> SelectModel: Empty / Next Model
    CheckEmpty --> ProcessRow: Has Rows
    
    ProcessRow --> ValidateRow: Get Next Row
    ValidateRow --> ProcessRow: Skip (Invalid)
    ValidateRow --> MapFields: Valid Row
    
    MapFields --> CheckRedisKey: Generate Key
    CheckRedisKey --> ReadExisting: Key Exists
    CheckRedisKey --> CreateNew: Key Not Found
    
    ReadExisting --> MergeData: Parse JSON
    CreateNew --> BuildValue: New Entry
    MergeData --> BuildValue: Merged Entry
    
    BuildValue --> WriteRedis: JSON Serialize
    WriteRedis --> ProcessRow: Write Complete
    
    ProcessRow --> QueryDatabase: Chunk Complete
    SelectModel --> Finished: All Models Done
    Finished --> [*]
```
